cgemv :: (Order) -> (Transpose) -> (Int) -> (Int) -> (Complex Float) -> (Ptr (Complex Float)) -> (Int) -> (Ptr (Complex Float)) -> (Int) -> (Complex Float) -> (Ptr (Complex Float)) -> (Int) -> IO ()
